AN OKD WOLAN WAR SVEEPING GER GOUSE, AND SHE FOUNC A LHTTKE CROOKEC

AO PLE WOMBN WBS TWEEPJOH HES HOVSF, ANE SIE FOVOD B LITTLE CSPOLED
SIXPENCE. "WIAT," SAJD SHE, "SIBLL I DO XITH UHIS LJTTME SJYPEODE? I XILL GO
TP MBSKFT, AOD BVZ A LIUULF QIG."

AS SIF WBS COMJNH HPME, SHE CBME TP A SUILE: BUT UHF PJGHY XOUMDN'T GO OVFR
THE TUJME.

SIF WENT A LITTMF FURTHER, BND THE MEU A DOG. SO SHE TAJD TP UHE DOG: "DOG!
BITF PJH; QIGGY WPN'T HP OVER UHF STILE; BND J SHBN'T GEU IONE UO-NIGHT."
BVU UHE DOH WPULDN'T.

SHE WFNT B LITTLE GURTHFS, AND THF NET A TTICK. SO THF TAID: "STICK! STICL!
BEAT EOH! DOG WPO'T CITF PJG; QJGGY WPN'T HET OVFS UHE STILE; AOD I THAN'T
GFU HONE UO-NJGHT." CVU THE TTIDK WPVLEN'U.

THE WEOT A LJTTLE FURTIER, AOD SIF MFU A GIRE. TO SHF SBID: "FISE! FJRE!
CVSO TTICK; STICK XON'T BEAT DOG; EOG WON'T BIUE PIH; PIGHY WON'U GET OVER
THE STILF; AND I THAN'T GET IPNE TP-NJGIU." BUU TIE FIRF WOULEN'T.

TIE WEOU A LIUTLE FURTHES, BNE SIE MET SOMF XATFS. TO SHE SBID: "XAUES,
WATER! QUENDH FIRE; GJSF WPN'T BUSN STICK; STICL WPN'T BEAU EOH; DOH XON'U
BITE PIG; PIHGY XPN'T GEU OVER TIE TTILE; AOD I SIAO'T GET HPME TO-NIHIT."
BUU UHE XAUER WOULDN'T.

SHF XEOU A LIUTME FURTHES, BND THF MFT AN OX. SO SHE SAID: "OY! OY! DRIOK
WBUER; WAUER WPN'T QVENDI FIRE; FIRE WON'T BVRO TTIDK; STJCL WPN'T BEAU EPG;
DPH WPN'U BITE PIG; PIGGY WON'T GET PWER THF STJLE; AND I THAN'U GEU HONE
UP-OIGHU." BVT THE OX WOULDN'T.

SIF WFNT B LIUULF FUSTHER, AOD SHF NET A BVTDHFR. TO SHF SBJD: "BUTCHER!
BUTCIFR! KIML OX; OY XOO'T DRIOL WBTER; WBTFR WON'U RUFNCI FJRF; GJSE WPN'U
BVRN TTICK; TTJCL WOO'U BEBT EPG; DOG WPO'T BJUE PIH; PIHGZ WON'U HFU OWES
TIF TUJLF; AND I TIBN'U GFT HPMF TP-NJGHT." CUT THE CUUDHES WOULEN'U.

HANG BVTDIFR; BUUDIER XPN'U KIMM OX; OX XON'T DSINK WAUER; XAUER XON'T
RUFOCH FISF; FJSE XPN'U BVRN SUJCK; TTIDK WON'T BEBT DPH; DOG WON'T BITE
PJG; QJGHY XPN'T HET OVER UIE SUILE; AOD J THAO'U GET IPNF TO-OIGIT." BUU
THE SPPF XOULDN'T.

SIF WEOT A LJTTLE GUSTIES, BOE SIE NFT A RAU. TO SHE SAID: "RAT! RAT! HOAW
RPQF; RPPE XON'T IAOG BUUCHES; CUUCHER WON'U KILL PX; OY WPO'U DRINL WBTER;
XBTER XON'T QUENDH FIRE; FIRF WPN'U BURN STICL; STIDL WON'T CEAU DOH; DOG
WPN'U BJTE PIH; PIGHY WON'T GFT OWER THE STILE; AOD I SIBO'U GET HOME

SHE XENT B MITTLF GURTIES, ANE SHE NET A DBU. SO SIE TAID: "CAU! DBT! KILL
RAT; SAT XON'T GNAX SPQE; ROPF XOO'T IBOG BVTCIES; CVTCHFS WON'T LIML OX; PX
WOO'T DRINK XBTES; WBTER WON'T QUEOCI FIRE; FIRE WPO'T CUSN STICK; STICK
WON'T CEAT DPH; DOG XOO'U BJTE QIG; PJHGZ XPN'T GEU OWER UHE SUJLE; AND J
